### [194] [Can Reinforcement Learning Efficiently Discover Price Manipulation?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06121)
*Ioanna-Yvonni Tsaknaki,Andrea Macrì,Fabrizio Lillo*

Main category: q-fin.TR

TL;DR: 本文研究模型无关的强化学习（RL）代理是否能比传统基于模型的方法更有效地发现和利用价格操纵机会。在Almgren-Chriss框架下，针对中等波动率市场，RL代理即使训练数据有限也能发现盈利的操纵策略，并在参数估计存在噪声时持续优于正确设定的模型方法；但在低波动率下模型方法更优，高波动率下所有方法均失效。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究在实际金融市场中，当模型参数估计存在噪声时，模型无关的强化学习方法是否比传统基于模型的方法更能有效识别和利用价格操纵机会。

Method: 在Almgren-Chriss框架下，先利用序贯最小二乘二次规划计算最优基准策略；再比较两种有限样本学习方法：基于模型的方法（从模拟交易数据估计冲击参数）和基于深度确定性策略梯度（DDPG）的强化学习方法，两者使用相同数据量进行训练。

Result: 中等波动率下，RL代理即使训练数据有限也能发现盈利的操纵策略，且在参数估计受采样误差影响时持续优于正确设定的模型方法；高波动率下所有方法均无法识别操纵机会；低波动率下模型方法优于RL。

Conclusion: RL在复杂控制问题中具有有效性，但也揭示了在金融市场部署学习算法时需设置适当安全措施的风险。

Abstract: In this paper, we investigate whether a model-free RL agent can identify and exploit price manipulation opportunities more effectively than a traditional model-based approach that assumes correct specification of the data-generating process but relies on noisy parameter estimates. We consider a single-asset market in which prices evolve according to an Almgren-Chriss framework with non-linear permanent impact and linear temporary impact. We first establish the existence of price-manipulative strategies in discrete time and compute the optimal benchmark strategy using Sequential Least Squares Quadratic Programming under full information. We then compare two finite-sample learning approaches: a model-based procedure that estimates impact parameters from simulated execution data and an agnostic RL approach based on Deep Deterministic Policy Gradient, trained directly on the same amount of data. For intermediate volatility, the RL agent successfully discovers profitable manipulative strategies without explicit knowledge of the underlying model, even when training data are quite limited. More importantly, RL consistently outperforms the model-based approach when parameter estimates are affected by sampling error, despite the latter benefiting from the correct model specification. For large volatility, all methods are unable to identify manipulation opportunities, while for small volatility, the model based approach outperforms RL. These findings highlight both the effectiveness of RL in complex control problems and the risks associated with deploying learning algorithms in financial markets without appropriate safeguards.

</details>

### [195] [Multimodal Video-to-Music Recommendation via Semantic Retrieval and Temporal Reranking](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05971)
*Seungheon Doh,Minhee Lee,Sangmoon Lee,Ben Sangbae Chon,Juhan Nam*

Main category: cs.MM

TL;DR: VTMR是一个两阶段视频到音乐推荐框架，第一阶段通过多模态检索对齐音视频文本信号并粗筛候选，第二阶段通过时序重排序捕捉细粒度对应关系，在R@10和Median Rank指标上显著超越基线，人类偏好评估与商业基线持平。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有视频到音乐推荐方法缺乏对视频与音乐之间语义兼容性和时序对应关系的有效建模，导致推荐质量不高。

Method: 两阶段框架：第一阶段在联合音视频文本表示空间中对齐信号，通过全局粗嵌入高效检索语义兼容候选；第二阶段按时序序列对检索结果进行重排序，捕捉细粒度时序对应。

Result: 多模态检索阶段R@10从14.2提升至15.9，Median Rank从75降至58；时序重排序进一步将R@10提升至18.3，Median Rank降至46。

Conclusion: VTMR通过多模态检索与时序重排序的互补结合显著提升视频到音乐推荐性能，人类偏好评估与商业基线相当，在音乐质量上优于生成式基线。

Abstract: We present VTMR, a two-stage framework for Video-To-Music Recommendation. In Stage~1, VTMR aligns comprehensive video and music signals in a joint audio-visual-text representation space and efficiently retrieves semantically compatible candidates using coarse global embeddings. In Stage~2, it reranks the retrieved candidates by attending to the temporal sequences of both video and music, thereby capturing fine-grained temporal correspondence. Evaluated on the video-to-music recommendation task, the multimodal retrieval stage improves R@10 from 14.2 to 15.9 and Median Rank from 75 to 58 over the strongest baseline; the temporal reranker further boosts R@10 to 18.3 and Median Rank to 46, demonstrating complementary gains from richer query encoding and temporal alignment. A human preference study confirms that VTMR is on par with a commercial baseline in overall preference, while outperforming a generative baseline in music quality.

### [196] [Precise Video-to-Audio Generation with Cross-Modal Alignment in Latent Space](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06405)
*Thanh V. T. Tran,Ngoc-Son Nguyen,Luong Tran,Long-Khanh Pham,Paarth Neekhara,Shezheen Hussain,Van Nguyen*

Main category: cs.MM

TL;DR: Flowley是一种端到端、单阶段训练的视频到音频生成架构，通过渐进式软掩码交叉注意力机制实现音视频同步，并配合SoundCap描述生成管道，在零样本设置下达到SOTA性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有V2A方法存在多阶段训练导致的高计算成本与长运行时间，或依赖文本转化而丢失细粒度时序信息的问题。

Method: 提出Flowley：单阶段端到端架构，结合视觉特征与文本提示；引入渐进式软掩码交叉注意力机制，无需额外计算成本即可嵌入音视频同步信息；提出SoundCap插件式管道，生成声音感知的详细描述以引导模型。

Result: 在VGGSound数据集上，Flowley无需任何预训练音视频对齐模块即达到多指标SOTA；结合SoundCap后，在零样本设置下的音频质量超越现有最强的闭源方法。

Conclusion: Flowley以更简洁高效的方式实现了高质量、同步的视频音频生成，表明端到端单阶段训练与内在注意力机制结合足以替代复杂的多阶段或文本中介方法。

Abstract: Video-to-audio (V2A) generation aims to synthesize realistic audio that is both semantically consistent with and temporally synchronized to a silent video. Despite recent progress, many methods still rely on multi-stage training, resulting in high computational costs and long runtimes, or transform visual input into text to leverage pretrained text-to-audio models, sacrificing fine-grained temporal cues. To overcome these limitations, we propose Flowley, an end-to-end, single-stage training architecture that produces soundtracks by combining visual features with textual prompts. Crucially, we introduce Progressive Soft-masked Cross-Attention, which embeds audio-visual synchronization directly within its attention mechanism, adding zero additional computational cost compared to standard attention layers. We further observe that existing V2A benchmarks lack sound-oriented descriptive captions, which can potentially degrade the quality of the synthesized audio. To remedy this, we propose SoundCap, a plug-and-play pipeline for creating detailed, sound-aware captions that guide the model. Remarkably, without integrating any pretrained audio-visual alignment modules, Flowley achieves state-of-the-art performance on VGGSound across multiple metrics. Moreover, by incorporating SoundCap, we further exceed the performance of the strongest existing close-sourced methods in terms of audio quality in the zero-shot setting.

### [197] [Relief-Gated Relative Rotation for QQQ-DIA Allocation: Globally Screened Relative States, Fixed Position Mapping, Incremental Interaction Admission, and Walk-Forward Validation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06117)
*Zheli Xiong*

Main category: q-fin.PM

TL;DR: 本文提出Relief-Gated Relative Rotation (RGRR)策略，是一种基于市场状态筛选的QQQ与DIA两ETF轮动规则，在计入10bps换手成本后，在2018、2020、2022三个样本外区间均改善了夏普比率，年化换手率高达354%-506%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统机械式轮动策略在极端市场环境下表现不佳，RGRR通过引入宏观缓解条件（利率、波动率、信用、大盘）对相对状态进行确认，旨在构建更具经济含义的、风险调整后的相对配置规则。

Method: 1) 全局筛选主效应与交互效应（通过HAC回归与相关性去重）；2) 固定信号集，仅滚动重新选择信号族lambda；3) 采用有界权重变换映射，构建包含1个主效应、9个二阶交互、2个三阶交互的最终模型；4) 计入10bps单边换手成本进行滚动样本外验证。

Result: 在2018、2020、2022三个样本外起点，RGRR在所有测试区间中夏普比率均优于100% QQQ和50/50 QQQ-DIA。CAGR方面优于50/50组合，但仅在2022窗口超越100% QQQ。2018年实现18.33% CAGR/0.94 Sharpe；2022年实现15.19% CAGR/0.87 Sharpe。

Conclusion: RGRR是一个有效的风险调整后相对配置规则，而非纯收益支配规则。其主要实际缺点是年化换手率极高（354%-506%），在实际执行中需考虑交易成本与执行可行性。

Abstract: This paper studies Relief-Gated Relative Rotation (RGRR), a two-ETF rule that allocates between QQQ and DIA by mapping screened relative and macro states into a continuous QQQ weight. RGRR is economic rather than mechanical: it rotates between a growth-heavy sleeve and a Dow/value-heavy sleeve only when QQQ-DIA relative states are confirmed by rate, volatility, credit, or broad-market relief conditions. Candidate main effects and interactions are globally screened with horizon-specific HAC regressions and correlation de-duplication, then held fixed during walk-forward validation. Rolling out-of-sample validation re-selects only signal-family lambdas, not the signal universe or the position mapping. The final stack contains one main effect, nine second-order interactions, and two third-order interactions. Third-order terms must also improve rolling out-of-sample Sharpe versus the main plus second-order base and survive economic-family de-duplication. The final mapping uses a fixed bounded weight transformation and includes a 10 bps one-way turnover cost.
  Across the 2018, 2020, and 2022 out-of-sample starts, RGRR improves Sharpe versus 100% QQQ and 50/50 QQQ-DIA in every tested interval. It improves CAGR versus 50/50 in every interval, but beats 100% QQQ on CAGR only in the 2022 window. In 2018, RGRR earns an 18.33% CAGR and 0.94 Sharpe, versus 20.50% and 0.89 for QQQ and 16.69% and 0.86 for 50/50. In 2022, it earns a 15.19% CAGR and 0.87 Sharpe, versus 14.65% and 0.70 for QQQ. The evidence supports RGRR as a risk-adjusted relative allocation rule, not a pure return-dominance rule. Its main practical weakness is high turnover, ranging from 354% to 506% annualized.

### [198] [Fast Alternating Radial Beamforming for Speed-of-Sound Imaging Based on Apparent Speckle Shifts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06244)
*Dieter Schweizer,Can Deniz Bezek,Orcun Goksel*

Main category: eess.IV

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有脉搏回波声速成像方法依赖笛卡尔网格波束形成，无法实现实时成像，且难以在资源有限、处理结构固定的传统超声系统中实现。

Method: 提出基于径向波束形成的资源高效方法，使用虚拟源发射实现实时波束形成；引入交替发射和快速配对交替波束形成技术，实现运动鲁棒的位移跟踪。

Result: 径向网格波束形成方法与笛卡尔网格方法性能相当，可在标准硬件上实现；声速数据采集帧率超过20 fps，可与常规B模式成像并行。

Conclusion: 所提出的基于散斑位移的径向方法结合快速交替波束形成，是实现标准超声系统上实时声速成像的重要一步。

Abstract: Pulse-echo speed-of-sound (SoS) imaging based on minute misalignments between consecutively acquired ultrasound images traditionally relies on images beamformed on Cartesian grids. Existing SoS imaging developments do not allow for real-time imaging and typically do not prioritize feasibility in conventional ultrasound systems that have limited resources and rigid processing structures. In this work, we propose a resource-efficient approach based on radial beamforming with virtual source transmits for implementation within an on-the-fly beamformer. We also introduce alternating transmissions with fast pair-alternating beamforming for motion-robust displacement tracking with typical line-based beamformers. We tested these methods comparatively on numerical simulations, tissue-mimicking phantom experiments, and in vivo data from breast lesion examinations. We demonstrate that the proposed radial grid beamforming approach performs comparably to a Cartesian grid approach, while allowing implementation on standard hardware for beamforming. Our proposed sequences would allow for SoS data acquisition frame rates of more than 20 fps in parallel to conventional B-mode imaging. The proposed speckle-shift based radial approach with fast alternation between congruent beamforming lines is a major step towards real-time SoS imaging on standard ultrasound systems with moderate resources.

### [199] [TMF-RSE: Tri-Modal Fusion with Regional Semantics and Evidential Uncertainty for Lung Severity Scoring](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06356)
*Fadi Abdeladhim Zidi,Salah Eddine Bekhouche,Abdellah Zakaria Sellam,Gaby Maroun,Fadi Dornaika,Cosimo Distante*

Main category: eess.IV

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种三模态深度学习框架TMF-RSE，结合胸部影像外观、肺部分割结构语义和视觉-语言模型特征，通过互补融合机制与证据回归，实现肺部疾病严重程度的精准量化与不确定性估计。在Per-COVID-19 CT和RALO数据集上，该方法在MAE和Pearson相关系数上均优于当前最先进的Transformer基线模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 胸部影像中肺部疾病严重程度的准确量化对于临床决策和资源分配至关重要，现有方法在跨模态信息融合与不确定性估计方面仍存在不足。

Method: 提出TMF-RSE三模态深度学习框架，融合2D胸部影像外观特征、肺部分割掩膜结构特征及视觉-语言模型语义特征，采用互补融合机制整合语义引导、结构先验和跨模态层次交互，并利用证据回归同时输出严重程度预测与不确定性估计。

Result: 在Per-COVID-19 CT数据集上MAE为4.02、Pearson相关系数为0.9629；在RALO数据集上地理范围预测MAE为0.339、Pearson相关系数为0.973，均优于近期Transformer基线方法。

Conclusion: TMF-RSE通过三模态融合与证据回归有效提升了肺部疾病严重程度量化的准确性，并能提供可靠的不确定性估计，具有重要的临床辅助价值。

Abstract: Accurate quantification of lung disease severity from chest imaging is critical for clinical decision-making and resource allocation. We propose a tri-modal deep learning framework, TMF-RSE (Tri-Modal Fusion with Regional Semantics and Evidential Uncertainty), that combines appearance features from two-dimensional chest inputs, structural features from lung segmentation masks, and semantic features from vision-language models (VLMs) for severity quantification. Our approach employs complementary fusion mechanisms that integrate semantic guidance, structural priors, and hierarchical interactions across modalities. The model employs evidential regression to provide both severity predictions and uncertainty estimates. Experiments on the Per-COVID-19 CT and RALO datasets show that TMF-RSE outperforms recent transformer-based baselines, achieving MAE of 4.02 and Pearson correlation of 0.9629 on Per-COVID-19 validation, and 0.339 MAE / 0.973 PC on RALO geographic extent.

</details>
